<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навеянный.html>наве́янный</a> (23873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***наводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a> (5207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навестить.html>навести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to direct <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to aim <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to point <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>след</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navodítʹ</b> na sled</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on the trail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navodítʹ</b> na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suggest an idea <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to somebody</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cover, to coat, to apply
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоск.html>лоск</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глянец.html>гля́нец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navodítʹ</b> losk, <b>navodítʹ</b> gljánec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gloss, to glaze, to veneer</span></div></dd>

<ol><li><i>(of a weapon)</i> laying, training

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наводчик.html>наво́дчик</a> (8054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводить.html>наводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводчик.html>наво́дчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navódčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводчик.html>наво́дчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводчик.html>наво́дчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наводчик.html>наво́дчиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наво́дчица</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gunlayer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tipper-off</li>
<li>person who finds a likely place for robbery, marker</li></ol>

***навоз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навоз.html>наво́з</a> (9860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воз.html>воз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally "something brought (on a cart)".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навоз.html>наво́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navóz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навоз.html>наво́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навоз.html>наво́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навоз.html>наво́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dung, manure</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">навозник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navoznik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***наворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наворачивать.html>навора́чивать</a> (28698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наворотить.html>навороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наворачивать.html>навора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наворотить.html>навороти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wind (something) up, to wrap (something) up circularly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heap up (a large quantity of something, in a disorderly way)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overcomplicate (something), to make (something) overly convoluted</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a mess of (something), to do (something undesirable or erroneous)</li></ol>

***наворотить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наворотить.html>навороти́ть</a> (19910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воротить.html>вороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наворотить.html>навороти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navorotítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наворачивать.html>навора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heap up (a large quantity of something, in a disorderly way)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overcomplicate (something), to make (something) overly convoluted</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a mess of (something), to do (something undesirable or erroneous)</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> сокурсниц <a href = vnd.unilang:протекать.html>протека́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурный.html>бу́рные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́ны</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дело</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:навороченный.html>наворо́ченных</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рках</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:врать.html>врать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наврать.html>навра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie <i>(to smb)</i>, to tell lies <i>(to smb)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:наврать.html>навра́ть</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:короб.html>короба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">navrátʹ s tri koroba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tell a pack of lies</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make mistakes <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наврать.html>навра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вычисление.html>вычисле́ниях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navrátʹ</b> v vyčislénijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go wrong in one's calculations; miscalculate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li></ol>
